DOCKERFILE:
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 node:22-bullseye
  # Install git and optional build dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git bash wget curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set working directory as per environment plan
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/vuejs_core
  # Install specific pnpm version globally
  RUN npm install -g pnpm@10.12.4
  # Copy lockfiles and package manifests first for better build caching
  COPY package.json pnpm-lock.yaml ./
  # Install dependencies using pnpm
  RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
  # Copy all remaining project files
  COPY . .
  # Set environment variables for Linux shell and Node.js
  ENV SHELL=/bin/bash
  ENV NODE_ENV=development
  # Expose default Vite/Node port
  EXPOSE 5173
  # Add healthcheck to verify that the dev server becomes ready
  HEALTHCHECK --interval=10s --timeout=5s --start-period=30s --retries=15 CMD wget --spider --quiet http://localhost:5173/ || exit 1
  # For debugging: start dev server in background and print process list
  RUN pnpm dev & sleep 10 && ps aux || true
  # Default command (can be overridden in docker-compose or at runtime)
  CMD ["pnpm", "dev"]

  - At runtime, the container fails due to a Node.js error: "Unknown option '--host'." This is thrown from a custom script (`scripts/dev.js`), not from Vite or a standard dev server.
  - The CMD in the Dockerfile passes `--host 0.0.0.0` unconditionally to `pnpm dev`, resulting in the error.
  - Environment variables, healthcheck, and port exposure are correctly set for a Linux dev workflow.
  next step
  - Investigate the `pnpm dev` script in the project's `package.json` to determine if it directly invokes a custom `scripts/dev.js` or another dev server.
  - If `pnpm dev` runs a custom Node.js script (not Vite or a tool that accepts `--host`), remove `--host 0.0.0.0` from the Dockerfile CMD and only include it if the underlying dev server supports it.
  - If the dev server is Vite or another tool that accepts `--host`, ensure `pnpm dev` is correctly configured to forward extra CLI arguments, or use environment variables (e.g., set `HOST=0.0.0.0` only).
  - Update the Dockerfile's CMD to match the actual supported options of the dev command, for example:
    - If custom script: `CMD ["pnpm", "dev"]`
    - If Vite: `CMD ["pnpm", "dev", "--host", "0.0.0.0"]`
  - Rebuild and retest the Docker container to confirm the runtime error is resolved.

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 node:22-bullseye
  # Install git and optional build dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git bash wget curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set working directory as per environment plan
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/vuejs_core
  # Install specific pnpm version globally
  RUN npm install -g pnpm@10.12.4
  # Copy lockfiles and package manifests first for better build caching
  COPY package.json pnpm-lock.yaml ./
  # Install dependencies using pnpm
  RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
  # Copy all remaining project files
  COPY . .
  # Set environment variables for Linux shell and Node.js
  ENV SHELL=/bin/bash
  ENV NODE_ENV=development
  ENV HOST=0.0.0.0
  # Expose default Vite/Node port
  EXPOSE 5173
  # Add healthcheck to verify that the dev server becomes ready
  HEALTHCHECK --interval=10s --timeout=5s --start-period=30s --retries=15 CMD wget --spider --quiet http://localhost:5173/ || exit 1
  # Default command (can be overridden in docker-compose or at runtime)
  CMD ["pnpm", "dev", "--", "--host", "0.0.0.0"]

  # Expose default Vite/Node port
  EXPOSE 5173

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 node:22-bullseye
  # Install git and optional build dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git bash wget curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set working directory as per environment plan
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/vuejs_core
  # Install specific pnpm version globally
  RUN npm install -g pnpm@10.12.4
  # Copy lockfiles and package manifests first for better build caching
  COPY package.json pnpm-lock.yaml ./
  # Install dependencies using pnpm
  RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
  # Copy all remaining project files
  COPY . .
  # Set environment variables for Linux shell and Node.js
  ENV SHELL=/bin/bash
  ENV NODE_ENV=development
  ENV HOST=0.0.0.0
  # Expose default Vite/Node port
  EXPOSE 5173
  # Add healthcheck to verify that the dev server becomes ready
  HEALTHCHECK --interval=10s --timeout=5s --start-period=30s --retries=15 CMD wget --spider --quiet http://localhost:5173/ || exit 1
  # Build step before starting dev server
  RUN pnpm build || true
  # Default command (can be overridden in docker-compose or at runtime)
  CMD pnpm dev -- --host 0.0.0.0

  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 node:22-bullseye
  # Install git and optional build dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git bash wget curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set working directory as per environment plan
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/vuejs_core
  # Install specific pnpm version globally
  RUN npm install -g pnpm@10.12.4
  # Copy lockfiles and package manifests first for better build caching
  COPY package.json pnpm-lock.yaml ./
  # Install dependencies using pnpm
  RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
  # Copy all remaining project files
  COPY . .
  # Set environment variables for Linux shell and Node.js
  ENV SHELL=/bin/bash
  ENV NODE_ENV=development
  ENV HOST=0.0.0.0
  # Expose default Vite/Node port
  EXPOSE 5173
  # Add healthcheck to verify that the dev server becomes ready
  HEALTHCHECK --interval=10s --timeout=5s --start-period=30s --retries=15 CMD wget --spider --quiet http://localhost:5173/ || exit 1
  # Build step before starting dev server
  RUN pnpm build || true
  # Default command (can be overridden in docker-compose or at runtime)
  CMD ["pnpm", "dev", "--host"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 node:22-bullseye
  # Install git and optional build dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git bash wget curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set working directory as per environment plan
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/vuejs_core
  # Install specific pnpm version globally
  RUN npm install -g pnpm@10.12.4
  # Copy lockfiles and package manifests first for better build caching
  COPY package.json pnpm-lock.yaml ./
  # Install dependencies using pnpm
  RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
  # Copy all remaining project files
  COPY . .
  # Set environment variables for Linux shell and Node.js
  ENV SHELL=/bin/bash
  ENV NODE_ENV=development
  ENV HOST=0.0.0.0
  # Expose default Vite/Node port
  EXPOSE 5173
  # Add healthcheck to verify that the dev server becomes ready
  HEALTHCHECK --interval=10s --timeout=5s --start-period=30s --retries=15 CMD wget --spider --quiet http://localhost:5173/ || exit 1
  # Build step before starting dev server
  RUN pnpm build || true
  # Default command (can be overridden in docker-compose or at runtime)
  CMD ["pnpm", "dev"]

  ENV NODE_ENV=development
  ENV HOST=0.0.0.0
  ENV VITE_HOST=0.0.0.0
  # Expose default Vite/Node port
  EXPOSE 5173
  # Add healthcheck to verify that the dev server becomes ready
  HEALTHCHECK --interval=10s --timeout=5s --start-period=30s --retries=15 CMD wget --spider --quiet http://localhost:5173/ || exit 1
  # Build step before starting dev server
  RUN pnpm build || true
  # Default command (can be overridden in docker-compose or at runtime)
  CMD ["pnpm", "dev", "--", "--host", "0.0.0.0"]
--- End of Iteration 22 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 node:22-bullseye
  # Install git and optional build dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git bash wget curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set working directory as per environment plan
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/vuejs_core
  # Install specific pnpm version globally
  RUN npm install -g pnpm@10.12.4
  # Copy lockfiles and package manifests first for better build caching
  COPY package.json pnpm-lock.yaml ./
  # Install dependencies using pnpm
  RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
  # Copy all remaining project files
  COPY . .
  # Set environment variables for Linux shell and Node.js
  ENV SHELL=/bin/bash
  ENV NODE_ENV=development
  ENV HOST=0.0.0.0
  ENV VITE_HOST=0.0.0.0
  # Expose default Vite/Node port
  EXPOSE 5173
  # Add healthcheck to verify that the dev server becomes ready
  HEALTHCHECK --interval=10s --timeout=5s --start-period=30s --retries=15 CMD wget --spider --quiet http://localhost:5173/ || exit 1
  # Build step before starting dev server
  RUN pnpm build || true
  # Default command (can be overridden in docker-compose or at runtime)
  CMD ["pnpm", "dev", "--host", "0.0.0.0"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 node:22-bullseye
  # Install git and optional build dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git bash wget curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set working directory as per environment plan
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/vuejs_core
  # Install specific pnpm version globally
  RUN npm install -g pnpm@10.12.4
  # Copy lockfiles and package manifests first for better build caching
  COPY package.json pnpm-lock.yaml ./
  # Install dependencies using pnpm
  RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
  # Copy all remaining project files
  COPY . .
  # Set environment variables for Linux shell and Node.js
  ENV SHELL=/bin/bash
  ENV NODE_ENV=development
  ENV HOST=0.0.0.0
  ENV VITE_HOST=0.0.0.0
  # Expose default Vite/Node port
  EXPOSE 5173
  # Add healthcheck to verify that the dev server becomes ready
  HEALTHCHECK --interval=10s --timeout=5s --start-period=30s --retries=15 CMD wget --spider --quiet http://localhost:5173/ || exit 1
  # Build step before starting dev server
  RUN pnpm build || true
  # Default command (can be overridden in docker-compose or at runtime)
  CMD ["pnpm", "dev"]

  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 node:22-bullseye
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git bash wget curl \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/vuejs_core

  COPY package.json pnpm-lock.yaml ./
  RUN pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
  COPY . .

  ENV NODE_ENV=development
  ENV HOST=0.0.0.0
  ENV VITE_HOST=0.0.0.0
  EXPOSE 5173
  HEALTHCHECK --interval=10s --timeout=5s --start-period=60s --retries=15 CMD wget --spider --quiet http://localhost:5173/ || exit 1
  RUN pnpm build || true
  CMD ["pnpm", "dev", "--host", "0.0.0.0"]

       - Required: >=18.12.0, ideally >=18.18.0 or >=20.0.0; must support Node.js 22.x for full compatibility (Netlify)

       - Required: v10.12.4 (ensure Linux x64 compatibility)

       - Verify: `pnpm -v`

       - Included with Node.js (Linux x64)

       - Latest stable version for Linux
       - Install via `apt-get install git` or `apk add git` in Docker; verify with `git --version`
